The piles should look like the figure to the right.\r\n\r\nThe four foundations (light rectangles in the upper right of the figure) are built up by suit from Ace (low in this game) to King, and the tableau piles can be built down by alternate colors, and partial or complete piles can be moved if they are built down by alternate colors also. Any empty piles can be filled with a King or a pile of cards with a King. The aim of the game is to build up a stack of cards starting with 2 and ending with King, all of the same suit. Once this is accomplished, the goal is to move this to a foundation, where the player has previously placed the Ace of that suit. card at a time, but placing no limit on passes through the deck.\r\nTurning three cards at once to the waste with no limit on passes through the deck, but allowing the player to switch once to a When matched, clears the entire column it is on.\r\n✓\tBy matching 4 jewels of the same color in one column and 3 jewels in one row or vice versa you get a cross buster. When matched, clears the entire row and column it is on.\r\n✓\tIf you are able to match 5 jewels, you get a super jewel. This can be switched with any other single jewel on the board. When activated, all the same-colored jewels as the jewel it was switched with, will be removed from the board. If you combine the jewel with a special jewel, all the jewels of that color will change into that special jewel, and activate those special jewels.\r\n✓\tBy matching 5 jewels of the same color in one column and 3 jewels in one row or vice versa you get a super cross jewel.
